uniform 	vec3 _WorldSpaceCameraPos;
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[4];
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[20];
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS

in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec3 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
float u_xlat9;
float u_xlat21;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy;
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat1.y * u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat1.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat9 = u_xlat21 * 0.125 + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat21 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat3.y = u_xlat21 + 0.125;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat9 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_4.xy = max(u_xlat3.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xy = u_xlat16_4.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_2 * _SHColorScale;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    u_xlat16_4.x = log2(abs(u_xlat0.y));
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_6.z = u_xlat16_4.x * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xz = exp2(u_xlat16_6.xz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = _AddlightLerp * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * 5.0 + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _AddlightAttenuation;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD8.y = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec3 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
float u_xlat9;
float u_xlat21;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy;
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat1.y * u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat1.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat9 = u_xlat21 * 0.125 + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat21 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat3.y = u_xlat21 + 0.125;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat9 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_4.xy = max(u_xlat3.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xy = u_xlat16_4.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_2 * _SHColorScale;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    u_xlat16_4.x = log2(abs(u_xlat0.y));
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_6.z = u_xlat16_4.x * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xz = exp2(u_xlat16_6.xz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = _AddlightLerp * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * 5.0 + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _AddlightAttenuation;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD8.y = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainLightShadowmapTexture;

vec3 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
uint u_xlatu0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
vec4 u_xlat6;
vec3 u_xlat7;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_7;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_8;
vec3 u_xlat9;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_9;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_10;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_11;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_12;
float u_xlat13;
uint u_xlatu13;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_15;
float u_xlat18;
float u_xlat22;
float u_xlat26;
int u_xlati26;
bool u_xlatb26;
mediump float u_xlat16_28;
float u_xlat39;
bool u_xlatb39;
float u_xlat40;
bool u_xlatb40;
mediump float u_xlat16_41;
mediump float u_xlat16_42;
mediump float u_xlat16_43;
float u_xlat44;
bool u_xlatb44;
float u_xlat45;
float u_xlat46;
mediump float u_xlat16_47;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_1.w + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_15.x = u_xlat16_0.w * u_xlat16_0.w + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_15.x = max(u_xlat16_15.x, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_15.x = min(u_xlat16_15.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -2.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(vec3(_NormalScale, _NormalScale, _NormalScale)) * u_xlat16_3.xyz + vec3(0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyw;
    u_xlat16_28 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_28 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_28);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_28) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_4.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_4.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat39 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat39 = max(u_xlat39, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat39 = inversesqrt(u_xlat39);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat39) * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(u_xlat6.xy,u_xlat6.z);
    u_xlat6.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(u_xlat7.xy,u_xlat7.z);
    u_xlat6.y = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    vec3 txVec2 = vec3(u_xlat7.xy,u_xlat7.z);
    u_xlat6.z = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec2, 0.0);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    vec3 txVec3 = vec3(u_xlat7.xy,u_xlat7.z);
    u_xlat6.w = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec3, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_28 = dot(u_xlat6, vec4(0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25));
    u_xlat16_41 = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_28 * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_41;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb40 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb40 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb44 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb44 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb40 = u_xlatb40 || u_xlatb44;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _MainlightAttenuation;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _InvRim;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec3 _AddLightDir;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SunShiftOffuse2;

in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec3 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
float u_xlat9;
float u_xlat21;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy;
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat1.y * u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat1.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat9 = u_xlat21 * 0.125 + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat21 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat3.y = u_xlat21 + 0.125;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat9 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_4.xy = max(u_xlat3.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xy = u_xlat16_4.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_2 * _SHColorScale;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    u_xlat16_4.x = log2(abs(u_xlat0.y));
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_6.z = u_xlat16_4.x * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xz = exp2(u_xlat16_6.xz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = _AddlightLerp * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * 5.0 + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _AddlightAttenuation;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD8.y = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainLightShadowmapTexture;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2DShadow hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture;

in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec4 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
bool u_xlatb0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
vec3 u_xlat7;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_8;
vec3 u_xlat9;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_10;
vec3 u_xlat11;
bool u_xlatb11;
float u_xlat12;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_13;
mediump float u_xlat16_14;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_17;
float u_xlat23;
float u_xlat34;
mediump float u_xlat16_35;
mediump float u_xlat16_36;
mediump float u_xlat16_37;
mediump float u_xlat16_39;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(u_xlat0.xy,u_xlat0.z);
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.y = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    vec3 txVec2 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.z = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec2, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    vec3 txVec3 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.w = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec3, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_2.x = dot(u_xlat0, vec4(0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25));
    u_xlat16_13.x = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_13.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb0 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb11 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb11 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlatb11 || u_xlatb0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (u_xlatb0) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat0.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_13.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_13.xyz = u_xlat16_13.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_13.xyz = min(u_xlat16_13.xyz, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -2.0);
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_0.w + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(vec3(_NormalScale, _NormalScale, _NormalScale)) * u_xlat16_3.xyz + vec3(0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_4.x);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xxx;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat11.x = log2(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat11.x = u_xlat11.x * _ShadowPow;
    u_xlat11.x = exp2(u_xlat11.x);
    u_xlat11.x = u_xlat11.x + _ShadowOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat11.x = min(max(u_xlat11.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat11.x = clamp(u_xlat11.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_13.xyz * u_xlat11.xxx;
    u_xlat16_13.xyz = max(u_xlat16_13.xyz, vec3(_ShadowScale));
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = max(u_xlat16_4.xyz, vec3(_ShadowScale));
    u_xlat16_5.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_5.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_5.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat11.x = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat11.x = max(u_xlat11.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat11.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat11.x);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat11.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat11.xyz = u_xlat11.xxx * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat34 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat34 = inversesqrt(u_xlat34);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat34) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat1.x = min(max(u_xlat1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat1.x = clamp(u_xlat1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat12 = (-u_xlat1.x) * u_xlat1.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_5 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_5.w * u_xlat16_5.w + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_37 = max(u_xlat16_37, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_37 = min(u_xlat16_37, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_37 * u_xlat16_37;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat16_6.x;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat1.x + u_xlat12;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat16_6.x / u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat12 = u_xlat16_6.x * u_xlat16_6.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat12 = float(1.0) / u_xlat12;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat23 = u_xlat16_37 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat23;
    u_xlat1.x = min(u_xlat1.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_36;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_6.x = min(max(u_xlat16_6.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_6.x = clamp(u_xlat16_6.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_36 = (-u_xlat16_36) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_36 = (-u_xlat16_36) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_36 = (-u_xlat16_37) + u_xlat16_36;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Emissive;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SunShiftOffuse1;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SunShiftOffuse2;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SunShift;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _specularColor1;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _glossiness_1X;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _glossiness_1Y;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _specularColor2;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _glossiness_2X;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _glossiness_2Y;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _shapeST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _ShadowScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _RimLightDir;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _faceshadowScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _FresnelColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _FresnelFactor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MainPlayerPositionWS;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _RampMap_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MatColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _MatMask;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SHColorScale;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec3 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
float u_xlat9;
float u_xlat21;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy;
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat1.y * u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat1.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat9 = u_xlat21 * 0.125 + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat21 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat3.y = u_xlat21 + 0.125;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat9 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_4.xy = max(u_xlat3.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xy = u_xlat16_4.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_2 * _SHColorScale;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    u_xlat16_4.x = log2(abs(u_xlat0.y));
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_6.z = u_xlat16_4.x * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xz = exp2(u_xlat16_6.xz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = _AddlightLerp * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * 5.0 + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _AddlightAttenuation;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD8.y = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainLightShadowmapTexture;

in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec4 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
bool u_xlatb0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
vec3 u_xlat7;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_8;
vec3 u_xlat9;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_10;
vec3 u_xlat11;
bool u_xlatb11;
float u_xlat12;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_13;
mediump float u_xlat16_14;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_17;
float u_xlat23;
float u_xlat34;
mediump float u_xlat16_35;
mediump float u_xlat16_36;
mediump float u_xlat16_37;
mediump float u_xlat16_39;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(u_xlat0.xy,u_xlat0.z);
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.y = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    vec3 txVec2 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.z = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec2, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    vec3 txVec3 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.w = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec3, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_2.x = dot(u_xlat0, vec4(0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25));
    u_xlat16_13.x = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_13.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb0 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb11 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb11 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlatb11 || u_xlatb0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (u_xlatb0) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat0.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_13.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_13.xyz = u_xlat16_13.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_13.xyz = min(u_xlat16_13.xyz, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -2.0);
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_0.w + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(vec3(_NormalScale, _NormalScale, _NormalScale)) * u_xlat16_3.xyz + vec3(0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_4.x);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xxx;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat11.x = log2(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat11.x = u_xlat11.x * _ShadowPow;
    u_xlat11.x = exp2(u_xlat11.x);
    u_xlat11.x = u_xlat11.x + _ShadowOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat11.x = min(max(u_xlat11.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat11.x = clamp(u_xlat11.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_13.xyz * u_xlat11.xxx;
    u_xlat16_13.xyz = max(u_xlat16_13.xyz, vec3(_ShadowScale));
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = max(u_xlat16_4.xyz, vec3(_ShadowScale));
    u_xlat16_5.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_5.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_5.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat11.x = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat11.x = max(u_xlat11.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat11.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat11.x);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat11.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat11.xyz = u_xlat11.xxx * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat34 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat34 = inversesqrt(u_xlat34);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat34) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat1.x = min(max(u_xlat1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat1.x = clamp(u_xlat1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat12 = (-u_xlat1.x) * u_xlat1.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_5 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_5.w * u_xlat16_5.w + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_37 = max(u_xlat16_37, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_37 = min(u_xlat16_37, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_37 * u_xlat16_37;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat16_6.x;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat1.x + u_xlat12;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat16_6.x / u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat12 = u_xlat16_6.x * u_xlat16_6.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat12 = float(1.0) / u_xlat12;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat23 = u_xlat16_37 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat23;
    u_xlat1.x = min(u_xlat1.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_36;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_6.x = min(max(u_xlat16_6.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_6.x = clamp(u_xlat16_6.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_36 = (-u_xlat16_36) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_36 = (-u_xlat16_36) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_36 = (-u_xlat16_37) + u_xlat16_36;
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_36 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_36 = min(max(u_xlat16_36, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_36 = clamp(u_xlat16_36, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xxx * u_xlat7.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = (-u_xlat16_5.xyz) * u_xlat16_6.xxx + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xzw = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xzw = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat1.xzw;
    u_xlat1.xzw = u_xlat1.xzw * _SpecularColor.xyz;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _AddlightDarkcolor;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _actorscale;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Mask;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _colorSkin;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _AddlightShadowScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _ActorScaleAttribute;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _ShadowOffset;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SunShiftOffuse1;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SunShiftOffuse2;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _specularColor1;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _glossiness_1X;

#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS

in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
float u_xlat8;
float u_xlat18;
float u_xlat19;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy;
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat1.y * u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat1.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat8 = u_xlat18 * 0.125 + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat18 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat3.y = u_xlat18 + 0.125;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat8 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_4.xy = max(u_xlat3.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xy = u_xlat16_4.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_2 * _SHColorScale;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0.xzw = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xzw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat0.xzw;
    u_xlat0.xzw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat0.xzw;
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat0.xzw, u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat0.xzw * vec3(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat1.x = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.xzw * u_xlat1.xxx;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = log2(abs(u_xlat0.y));
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_5.z = u_xlat16_4.x * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xz = exp2(u_xlat16_5.xz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = _AddlightLerp * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * 5.0 + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _AddlightAttenuation;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD8.y = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;

in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;

in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec2 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
uint u_xlatu0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
vec3 u_xlat7;
vec3 u_xlat8;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_8;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_9;
vec3 u_xlat10;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_11;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_12;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_13;
float u_xlat14;
uint u_xlatu14;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_16;
float u_xlat19;
float u_xlat24;
float u_xlat28;
int u_xlati28;
bool u_xlatb28;
mediump float u_xlat16_30;
float u_xlat42;
bool u_xlatb42;
float u_xlat43;
mediump float u_xlat16_44;
mediump float u_xlat16_45;
mediump float u_xlat16_46;
float u_xlat47;
mediump float u_xlat16_48;
float u_xlat49;
float u_xlat50;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_1.w + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_16.x = u_xlat16_0.w * u_xlat16_0.w + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_16.x = max(u_xlat16_16.x, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_16.x = min(u_xlat16_16.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -2.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(vec3(_NormalScale, _NormalScale, _NormalScale)) * u_xlat16_3.xyz + vec3(0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyw;
    u_xlat16_30 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_30 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_30);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_30) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_4.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_4.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat42 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat42 = max(u_xlat42, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat42 = inversesqrt(u_xlat42);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat42) * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_30 = (-u_xlat16_2.x) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_30 = (-u_xlat16_30) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_2.x = min(max(u_xlat16_2.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_2.x = clamp(u_xlat16_2.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = (-u_xlat16_0.xyz) * u_xlat16_2.xxx + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * u_xlat7.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_2.x = (-u_xlat16_16.x) + u_xlat16_30;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_2.x = min(max(u_xlat16_2.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_2.x = clamp(u_xlat16_2.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_30 = u_xlat16_16.x * u_xlat16_16.x;
    u_xlat43 = u_xlat16_30 * u_xlat16_30;
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * vec3(u_xlat42) + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat42 = dot(u_xlat8.xyz, u_xlat8.xyz);
    u_xlat42 = inversesqrt(u_xlat42);
    u_xlat8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat42) * u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat42 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat42 = min(max(u_xlat42, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat42 = clamp(u_xlat42, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_44 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_44 = abs(u_xlat16_44) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_44 = min(u_xlat16_44, 1.0);
    u_xlat47 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat8.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat47 = min(max(u_xlat47, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat47 = clamp(u_xlat47, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat49 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat8.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat49 = min(max(u_xlat49, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat49 = clamp(u_xlat49, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_45 = dot((-u_xlat1.xyz), u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_45 = u_xlat16_45 + u_xlat16_45;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_45)) + (-u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat8.x = (-u_xlat16_44) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_45 = u_xlat8.x * u_xlat8.x;
    u_xlat16_45 = u_xlat16_45 * u_xlat16_45;
    u_xlat16_46 = (-u_xlat16_16.x) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_46 = u_xlat16_16.x * u_xlat16_46;
    u_xlat16_46 = u_xlat16_46 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_4 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_46);
    u_xlat16_48 = u_xlat16_4.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_48 = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_48 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_48 = max(u_xlat16_48, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_48 = log2(u_xlat16_48);
    u_xlat16_48 = u_xlat16_48 * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_48 = exp2(u_xlat16_48);
    u_xlat16_48 = u_xlat16_48 * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_48);
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat16_30 * u_xlat16_30 + 1.0;
    u_xlat8.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat8.x;
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * u_xlat8.xxx;
    u_xlat10.xyz = (-u_xlat7.xyz) + u_xlat16_2.xxx;
    u_xlat10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_45) * u_xlat10.xyz + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat8.xyz * u_xlat10.xyz;
    u_xlat8.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz * u_xlat16_6.xyz + u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat50 = log2(u_xlat42);
    u_xlat50 = u_xlat50 * _ShadowPow;
    u_xlat50 = exp2(u_xlat50);
    u_xlat50 = u_xlat50 + _ShadowOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat50 = min(max(u_xlat50, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat50 = clamp(u_xlat50, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat10.x = (-u_xlat47) * u_xlat47 + 1.0;
    u_xlat24 = u_xlat16_30 * u_xlat47;

    vs_TEXCOORD8.xz = exp2(u_xlat16_5.xz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = _AddlightLerp * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * 5.0 + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _AddlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.y = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
#define UNITY_UNIFORM
#else
#define UNITY_UNIFORM uniform
#endif
#define UNITY_SUPPORTS_UNIFORM_LOCATION 1
#if UNITY_SUPPORTS_UNIFORM_LOCATION
#define UNITY_LOCATION(x) layout(location = x)
#define UNITY_BINDING(x) layout(binding = x, std140)
#else
#define UNITY_LOCATION(x)
#define UNITY_BINDING(x) layout(std140)
#endif
uniform 	vec3 _WorldSpaceCameraPos;
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[4];
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
UNITY_BINDING(0) uniform UnityPerDraw {
#endif
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[4];
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[4];
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_LODFade;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_WorldTransformParams;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_LightData;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_LightIndices[2];
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_ProbesOcclusion;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SpecCube0_HDR;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_LightmapST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_DynamicLightmapST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHAr;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHAg;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHAb;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHBr;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHBg;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHBb;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHC;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
UNITY_BINDING(1) uniform UnityPerMaterial {
#endif
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MainTex_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _HairMap_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _BumpMapNr2_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RoughNessOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SpecularColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _MetallicOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _NormalScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SHScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SHTopColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SHBotColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _MainlightAttenuation;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _InvRim;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec3 _AddLightDir;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _AddlightColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _AddlightDarkcolor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _AddlightScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _AddlightAttenuation;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _AddlightLerp;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RimlightScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RimlightScale2;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RimlightShadowScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _RimlightColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RimlightAttenuation;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _actorscale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Cutoff;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _BumpScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Mask;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _colorSkin;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _AddlightShadowScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _ActorScaleAttribute;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _ShadowOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _ShadowPow;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _EmisssionScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Emissive;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SunShiftOffuse1;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SunShiftOffuse2;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SunShift;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _specularColor1;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _glossiness_1X;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _glossiness_1Y;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _specularColor2;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _glossiness_2X;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _glossiness_2Y;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _shapeST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _ShadowScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _RimLightDir;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _faceshadowScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _FresnelColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _FresnelFactor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MainPlayerPositionWS;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _RampMap_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MatColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _MatMask;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SHColorScale;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
float u_xlat8;
float u_xlat18;
float u_xlat19;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy;
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat1.y * u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat1.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat8 = u_xlat18 * 0.125 + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat18 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat3.y = u_xlat18 + 0.125;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat8 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_4.xy = max(u_xlat3.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xy = u_xlat16_4.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_2 * _SHColorScale;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0.xzw = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xzw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat0.xzw;
    u_xlat0.xzw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat0.xzw;
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat0.xzw, u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat0.xzw * vec3(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat1.x = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.xzw * u_xlat1.xxx;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = log2(abs(u_xlat0.y));
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_5.z = u_xlat16_4.x * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xz = exp2(u_xlat16_5.xz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = _AddlightLerp * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * 5.0 + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _AddlightAttenuation;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD8.y = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

#endif

uniform 	vec4 _MainLightPosition;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _MainLightColor;

uniform 	mediump float _ShineRoughness;
uniform 	mediump vec3 _ShineColor1;

#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS

};
#endif
UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMapNr;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _ShiningBump;
UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _ShineMask;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec2 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
vec3 u_xlat7;
vec3 u_xlat8;
vec3 u_xlat9;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_10;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_11;
vec3 u_xlat12;
mediump float u_xlat16_13;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_14;
float u_xlat15;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_18;
mediump float u_xlat16_26;
mediump float u_xlat16_37;
mediump float u_xlat16_38;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -2.0);
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_0.w + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(vec3(_NormalScale, _NormalScale, _NormalScale)) * u_xlat16_1.xyz + vec3(0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_2.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_2.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xxx;
    u_xlat16_2.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_2.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_2.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat12.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.x = dot((-u_xlat12.xyz), u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x + u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * (-u_xlat16_2.xxx) + (-u_xlat12.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_4.w * u_xlat16_4.w + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_38 = max(u_xlat16_38, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_38 = min(u_xlat16_38, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_5.x = (-u_xlat16_38) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_38 * u_xlat16_5.x;
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_5 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_5.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_2.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = max(u_xlat16_2.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_2.x = log2(u_xlat16_2.x);
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_2.x = exp2(u_xlat16_2.x);
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xxx;
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_38 * u_xlat16_38;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_6.x * u_xlat16_6.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat0.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx;
    u_xlat16_2.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat12.xyz);
    u_xlat16_2.x = abs(u_xlat16_2.x) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_2.x = min(u_xlat16_2.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat0.x = (-u_xlat16_2.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_14.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat16_14.x = u_xlat16_14.x * u_xlat16_14.x;
    u_xlat16_2.z = (-u_xlat16_37) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_37;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_37 = min(max(u_xlat16_37, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_37 = clamp(u_xlat16_37, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_2.xz = (-u_xlat16_2.xz) + vec2(1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_26 = (-u_xlat16_38) + u_xlat16_2.z;
    u_xlat16_26 = u_xlat16_26 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_26 = min(max(u_xlat16_26, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_26 = clamp(u_xlat16_26, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_37) * u_xlat8.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_18.xyz = (-u_xlat16_4.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_37) + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_26) + (-u_xlat8.xyz);
    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat16_14.xxx * u_xlat9.xyz + u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat7.xyz * u_xlat9.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz * u_xlat16_18.xyz + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);

    u_xlat18 = u_xlat18 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat3.y = u_xlat18 + 0.125;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat8 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_4.xy = max(u_xlat3.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xy = u_xlat16_4.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_2 * _SHColorScale;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0.xzw = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xzw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat0.xzw;
    u_xlat0.xzw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat0.xzw;
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat0.xzw, u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat0.xzw * vec3(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat1.x = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.xzw * u_xlat1.xxx;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = log2(abs(u_xlat0.y));
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_5.z = u_xlat16_4.x * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xz = exp2(u_xlat16_5.xz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = _AddlightLerp * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * 5.0 + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _AddlightAttenuation;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD8.y = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;

    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx;
    u_xlat16_2.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat12.xyz);
    u_xlat16_2.x = abs(u_xlat16_2.x) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_2.x = min(u_xlat16_2.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat0.x = (-u_xlat16_2.x) + 1.0;

    u_xlat16_14.x = u_xlat16_14.x * u_xlat16_14.x;

#else

    u_xlat16_14.xyz = u_xlat7.xyz + u_xlat16_14.xyz;
    u_xlat16_37 = dot(_AddLightDir.xyz, _AddLightDir.xyz);
    u_xlat16_37 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_37);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_37) * _AddLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat16_37 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat16_6.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_37 = min(max(u_xlat16_37, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_37 = clamp(u_xlat16_37, 0.0, 1.0);

    u_xlat16_6.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_37) * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_14.xyz * u_xlat16_6.xyz;

    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat16_14.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = _MainLightPosition.xyz * vec3(0.400000006, 0.400000006, 0.400000006) + u_xlat12.xyz;
